[30;1m36 | [0m[35m.. important::[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35m    Tenant's domain name and schema name are usually the same or similar but they don't have to be![0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35m    For example the tenant at http://acme.example.com could be backed by the ``acme`` schema, while[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35m    http://looney-tunes.tld could be backed by the ``tenant2`` schema!  Notice that domain names are[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35m    not related in any way to schema names! There is also no restriction whether or not you should[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35m    use sub-domains or top-level domains.[0m
